<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:this.html>This</a> etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:missing.html>missing</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:incomplete.html>incomplete</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:please.html>Please</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:add.html>add</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:it.html>it</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:discuss.html>discuss</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:it.html>it</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:at.html>at</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> Etymology scriptorium.)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:jeuken.html>jeuken</a> (19848)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">joken</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">juecken</i>, long-vowel variants <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">jocken</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">jucken</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:juk.html>jukken</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*jukjaną</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>The</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:long.html>long</a> vowels developed <a href = vnd.unilang:before.html>before</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:single.html>single</a> consonants <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> 2nd <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> 3rd <a href = vnd.unilang:person.html>person</a> singular forms, <a href = vnd.unilang:e.html>e</a>.<a href = vnd.unilang:g.html>g</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a> 3rd <a href = vnd.unilang:person.html>person</a> singular <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*jukit</i>.
</p><p>Cognate <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">jucken</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language"><a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:itch.html>itch</a></i>.

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:ji.html>ji</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:northern.html>northern</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:form.html>form</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:gi.html>gi</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">gī</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*jīz</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:northwest.html>northwest</a> Germanic <a href = vnd.unilang:variant.html>variant</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*jūz</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*yū́</i>. ***jinx.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:jinx.html>jinx</a> (35982)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">jynx</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <span class="Latn" lang="en">transferred <a href = vnd.unilang:sense.html>sense</a></span> “a <a href = vnd.unilang:charm.html>charm</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> spell”.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:jinx.html>jinx</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">jinxes</b>)
</p>
